Easy place to lose track of time. I come when the lights are on and stay well into  them turning the lights off. Bowling and pool is a beautiful combination. The crowd that comes here keeps the venue exciting. The later into the day you stay the wilder it gets. It‚Äôs a party up in here. I always have a lot of fun when I visit. The competition really shows up here.  It‚Äôs all fun and games until someone bowls a 279

I‚Äôve been practicing and I‚Äôm considering joining a league soon. People come at all skill levels, but I see a bunch of great bowlers here regularly. Sweet place to be at during the week or on the weekend. Can‚Äôt go wrong.<//Review>

<date>1555653535427< /date><Pics>None< /Pics><gmapID>0x80945d1f96be0d41:0xeb88c714c179c87f< /gmapID><text>I have not been here in years but this place is just as good as I remember. They even added a lift for the handicapped individuals who want to bowl and I thought that was cool. This place is welcoming and you really have no reason not to have a good time here, unless you're by yourself. They also have billiards and arcade games here as well. The food is what you would expect. The public prices are reasonable, and some of the shoe rentals are very old and some are newer but both work. There were plenty of bowling balls when I went but if multiple Lanes were filled there might've been a shortage but not by much. I also observed that the scoring was a bit off at times. We brought a child and he was able to use the bumper lane and the other bowling helper. I am glad that I finally made it back to this alley.< /text>< response>

< text>
Let's get a few things out of the way. My review is based on my experience. I've been going to Newport course for a couple of months,  that's when i started playing golf. The driving range is fantastic and usually pretty quiet 6:30am when I go. The putting green is great and free to use. The course is small,  mostly par 3's and will have you walking in all kinds of directions along the way. By no means is this the best course of played on however i don't need to book to play,  i can play by myself,  the staff are always very friendly,  accommodating and polite and I've made friends there that i can play with every week. Don't go expecting a par 72 course but appreciate being able to play alone of you wish and be ready to make new friends!<//text>

< text>
Love Newport Rubber Mats!
I've been playing golf here since 2005 & the course had changed a lot since then.

1st - It's one of the only executive courses in the area that I know of - other than David L Baker in Fountain Valley. (Executive Courses, for those that don't know: have only Par 3 & Par 4 holes. No 5s. Holes range from 80ish yards to about 260).

2nd - they now have golf carts, some holes you can even hit off grass, they took down the massive & annoying fence on the 4th hole & some of the holes even have a couple T'boxes you can choose to hit from.

The price has gone up since they got golf carts & have some T'boxes on grass... All done after the new owner took over.

Honestly, I always thought it was a cheap price for what it is, so I'm glad they hiked up their prices... To a degree. They deserved more, but even with the golf cart price added in to the green fees, now, it is just a litttttttle bit over-priced for what the course is.

**I know that's a back/forth statement about the Course's pricing but I had to mention it, at the least.
Yes, I think the price shouldve gone up. But since the prices are higher, the golf carts & T'boxes don't justify it. In my mind - the price should be reflected on the course's maintenance. And a lot of the course isn't very well maintained. **I must say here -- I still love this course! It's fun. Hole layout is fun. Some holes are quite challenging. *It's just... the fairways, areas surrounding the greens & even some greens specifically... Theres dead grass (more so than I remember), a lot of areas where they either don't want to maintain or choose to "let go" & it's just like someone's poorly maintained backyard...

All that said -- It's not toooo Expensive. It's just a couple dollars over-priced for having not very well-maintained the full course.

Fortunately for Newport Golf Course, none of this/my opinion matters. They seem to be busy anyway & I'm happy they are! I just hope, after they take that higher income for a while, that they'll maintain the course a little better... And then NOT bike the price again :-)

Either which way shape or form - I'll be golfing here for many more years to come... Unless the price goes so far that I could play a full course for the same price.</text>

<Resp>None<//Resp>< Review>
This is a great short course. For the most part, you're hitting off grass (except for the mat tee boxes) since they do a pretty good job of course maintenance. Great for beginner players as there isn't a lot of water or huge sand traps. You can get through the course pretty quickly so you don't have to spend 4+ hours at the course. May want to purchase a tee adapter from them for $2 so that you can use your tees on the par 4's. My wife is a beginner and has enjoyed learning to play golf on this course.</Review>

< text>
(Translated by Google) This Newport Beach Golf Course is located next to JOHN Wayne Airport. What makes it special is its 18-hole golf course, which has only five par fours and the rest are par three with a total of 59. It is a venue for training and demonstrating short-strap skills. 1450421172945</time>

< text>
Very highly recommended. This location is "new" - that is, although the buildings have been here for some time, the property has only just recently become part of the Extra Space brand...and they've done a thorough facelift on the place. I've been to a number of self storage places over the years, including some other ExtraSpace locations, and they always feel vaguely horror-movie-ish...long,  scary hallways with flickering light bulbs, rusty elevators and creaky doors. Not so at this place. SUPER clean, well-lit hallways inside AND plenty of floodlights outside, and freshly painted. Units are odor free, individually alarmed, and well lit  also.

My only suggestion is adding doorstops at the hallway entrances, and smoothing out the transitions from the ground outside to the concrete floor of the hallways...as it is, the slight lip of the concrete sometimes makes it difficult to roll a hand truck through the door.

Keep it up!<//text>
